FE-04 - Log out
TC-01Test Logout with valid refresh token1. Login to the system with a valid account that can access this feature.
2. Open the account menu or settings screen.
3. Perform the scenario with the required data: refreshToken=valid.refresh.token.
4. Click the Logout button.

3. Enter the form data for this scenario: {"user_id": "11111111-1111-1111-1111-111111111111", "seat_id": "12", "start_time": "2026-04-10T08:00:00", "end_time": "2026-04-10T10:00:00"}.
4. Click the Save/Submit button.
5. Observe the system result on the current screen.		200: OK
The system saves the data successfully and shows the corresponding success result.
The booking information is displayed with the newly created reservation details.		The user is logged in with a valid student account.
The user is authenticated in the system.		Passed2026-04-09
